<h2>Flowers Dedicated to the Celebration of Mum&#x27;s Day Across the World</h2>
<p>No doubt, there are varieties of flowers for mothers day that can be selected for the occasion but it is important to choose the right flowers based on the choice of colour, fragrance and their associated meanings. Let us throw some light on the blooms for the mom&#x27;s day that can be sent as mothers day flowers delivery in India as well as abroad.</p>
<h3>Carnations</h3>
<p>They are the most traditional flowers for mum&#x27;s day and are available in different colours. Pink Carnations are known to signify the gratitude and love towards your mommy while red carnations stand for the admiration of her. White Carnations are given in the loving memory of a mom who is not alive anymore. Choose any varieties of carnations and express your emotions towards the mother in a unique manner.</p>
<h3>Roses</h3>
<p>There is a special meaning attached to every rose bloom depending on their colour types. While mature rose blooms offer a message of gratitude, it is hard to find the best coloured rose for mother&#x27;s day. The white roses signify virtue, purity and reverence, yellow roses are a symbol of devotion, medium pink blooms refer to grace, dark pink hues signify gratitude whereas the light pink hues mean youthful joy. So, which happy Mother&#x27;s Day roses do you plan on giving to her?</p>
<h3>Sunflowers and Gerbera Daisies</h3>
<p>Gifting sunflower as mum&#x27;s day flower is a wonderful way to spread cheerfulness and smile in the lives of your mother. The flower also signifies the admiration and respect for the beloved mom. Gerbera Daisies are also a great option for buying mothers day flowers due to their exciting colours. Daisies represent the beauty while the gerbera signifies the cheerfulness and playfulness.</p>
<h3>Tulips</h3>
<p>Send mother&#x27;s day flowers delivery to India in the form of this eye grabbing bouquet of tulips that can seamlessly make the day of your beloved mommy. Tulips in general show love, whereas the pink tulips refer to the caring spirit, red tulips denote the true love and yellow tulips bring the thought of cheerfulness.</p>
<h3>Lilies</h3>
<p>They are one of the most loved happy mothers day flowers that arrive in multiple colours. The white lily denotes the purity and majesty whereas the Calla lilies refer to the beauty. Similarly, the day lily is a Chinese symbol of motherhood.</p>
<h3>Violets</h3>
<p>The flower signifies the faithfulness and devotion of a mother. Gifting violet flower to your mum would serve as an everlasting reminder of her devotion.</p>
<h3>Orchids</h3>
<p>Orchids are known for their exotic and magical appearance which symbolises love, refinement and beauty. The flower is a Chinese symbol of &quot;many children&quot;.</p>
<p>Not just that, there are other spring flowers such as Narcissus, Tulips, Daffodils, Muscari, Hyacinths, Primrose, Lily of the Valley, Peonies, Spiraea, Lilac, Wood Anemone and others that can together form a wonderful spring bouquets for your mom. You could even explore gifting the special designer bouquet known as &quot;Mum&#x27;s Charm&quot; to celebrate the mom&#x27;s day in an exotic manner. </p>
